\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This function is used to change the I2C address of the sensor. If multiple VL53\+L5 sensors are connected to the same I2C line, all other LPn pins needs to be set to Low. The default sensor address is 0x52. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This function is used to set the sensor in Low Power mode, for example if the sensor is not used during a long time. The macro VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+POWER\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+SLEEP can be used to enable the low power mode. When user want to restart the sensor, he can use macro VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+POWER\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+WAKEUP. Please ensure that the device is not streaming before calling the function. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This function is used to check if the synchronization pin is enabled or disabled. When it is enabled, the sensor waits an interrupt on B1 pin to start the next measurement. It is useful for multi-\/devices synchronization. By default the sync pin is disabled. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
uint8\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a5a7e192664394511227839bca8f2ea30}{vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+external\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin\+\_\+enable}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev, uint8\+\_\+t enable\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This function is used to enable or disable the synchronization pin. When it is enabled, the sensor waits an interrupt on B1 pin to start the next measurement. It is useful for multi-\/devices synchronization. By default the sync pin is disabled. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This function is used to set a periodic temperature compensation. By setting a repeat count different to 0 the firmware automatically runs a temperature calibration every N frames. default the repeat count is set to 0. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

uint8\+\_\+t \+\_\+vl53l8cx\+\_\+poll\+\_\+for\+\_\+answer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{size}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{pos}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{address}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{mask}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{expected\+\_\+value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Inner function, not available outside this file. This function is used to wait for an answer from VL53\+L8\+CX sensor. 

Copyright (c) 2021 STMicroelectronics. All rights reserved.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a8d192f0f3fded5de1767f54271d8f54a} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+check\+\_\+data\+\_\+ready (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+is\+Ready}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function checks if a new data is ready by polling I2C. If a new data is ready, a flag will be raised. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint8\+\_\+t)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+is\+Ready \+: Value of this pointer be updated to 0 if data is not ready, or 1 if a new data is ready. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if I2C reading is OK 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a622e5a7b1ab7b329bb6eee40429599da} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+dci\+\_\+read\+\_\+data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{index}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{data\+\_\+size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function can be used to read \textquotesingle{}extra data\textquotesingle{} from DCI. Using a known index, the function fills the casted structure passed in argument. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint8\+\_\+t)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}data \+: This field can be a casted structure, or a simple array. Please note that the FW only accept data of 32 bits. So field data can only have a size of 32, 64, 96, 128, bits .... \\
\hline
{\em (uint32\+\_\+t)} & index \+: Index of required value. \\
\hline
{\em (uint16\+\_\+t)\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}data\+\_\+size} & \+: This field must be the structure or array size (using sizeof() function). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if OK 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_get\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable()}{vl53l8cx\_get\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a93e5eea91d745d39ddf7788f2767abff} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+get\+\_\+external\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin\+\_\+enable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+is\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin\+\_\+enabled}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function is used to check if the synchronization pin is enabled or disabled. When it is enabled, the sensor waits an interrupt on B1 pin to start the next measurement. It is useful for multi-\/devices synchronization. By default the sync pin is disabled. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint8\+\_\+t\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})} & p\+\_\+is\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin\+\_\+enabled \+: Pointer of sync pin status. Value overridden to 0 if the pin is disabled, or 1 if the pin is enabled. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if get sync pin OK. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a5a7e192664394511227839bca8f2ea30}\index{vl53l8cx\_api.c@{vl53l8cx\_api.c}!vl53l8cx\_set\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable@{vl53l8cx\_set\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable}}
\index{vl53l8cx\_set\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable@{vl53l8cx\_set\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable}!vl53l8cx\_api.c@{vl53l8cx\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_set\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable()}{vl53l8cx\_set\_external\_sync\_pin\_enable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a5a7e192664394511227839bca8f2ea30} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+external\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin\+\_\+enable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{enable\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function is used to enable or disable the synchronization pin. When it is enabled, the sensor waits an interrupt on B1 pin to start the next measurement. It is useful for multi-\/devices synchronization. By default the sync pin is disabled. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint8\+\_\+t)} & enable\+\_\+sync\+\_\+pin \+: Ste the value to 1 to enable the sync pin, or 0 to disable it. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if set sync pin OK. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_set\_i2c\_address()}{vl53l8cx\_set\_i2c\_address()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a705b4dd09a2ae3c873b6f5896bb999dc} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+i2c\+\_\+address (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{i2c\+\_\+address}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function is used to change the I2C address of the sensor. If multiple VL53\+L5 sensors are connected to the same I2C line, all other LPn pins needs to be set to Low. The default sensor address is 0x52. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint16\+\_\+t)} & i2c\+\_\+address \+: New I2C address. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if new address is OK 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{vl53l8cx\_set\_integration\_time\_ms@{vl53l8cx\_set\_integration\_time\_ms}!vl53l8cx\_api.c@{vl53l8cx\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_set\_integration\_time\_ms()}{vl53l8cx\_set\_integration\_time\_ms()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_abcb4f3ccc4813f4aa1851c2d5844641a} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+integration\+\_\+time\+\_\+ms (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{integration\+\_\+time\+\_\+ms}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function sets a new integration time in ms. Integration time must be computed to be lower than the ranging period, for a selected resolution. Please note that this function has no impact on ranging mode continous. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint32\+\_\+t)} & time\+\_\+ms \+: Contains the integration time in ms. For all resolutions and frequency, the minimum value is 2ms, and the maximum is 1000ms. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if set integration time is OK. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{vl53l8cx__api_8c_affb39664fa0b0d1e37c49ab7725a3ce4}\index{vl53l8cx\_api.c@{vl53l8cx\_api.c}!vl53l8cx\_set\_power\_mode@{vl53l8cx\_set\_power\_mode}}
\index{vl53l8cx\_set\_power\_mode@{vl53l8cx\_set\_power\_mode}!vl53l8cx\_api.c@{vl53l8cx\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_set\_power\_mode()}{vl53l8cx\_set\_power\_mode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_affb39664fa0b0d1e37c49ab7725a3ce4} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+power\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{power\+\_\+mode}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function is used to set the sensor in Low Power mode, for example if the sensor is not used during a long time. The macro VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+POWER\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+SLEEP can be used to enable the low power mode. When user want to restart the sensor, he can use macro VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+POWER\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+WAKEUP. Please ensure that the device is not streaming before calling the function. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint8\+\_\+t)} & power\+\_\+mode \+: Selected power mode (VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+POWER\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+SLEEP or VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+POWER\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+WAKEUP) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if power mode is OK, or 127 if power mode requested by user is not valid. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{vl53l8cx__api_8c_aa498a79da766ce9f30d4518403bfbc96}\index{vl53l8cx\_api.c@{vl53l8cx\_api.c}!vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_frequency\_hz@{vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_frequency\_hz}}
\index{vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_frequency\_hz@{vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_frequency\_hz}!vl53l8cx\_api.c@{vl53l8cx\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_frequency\_hz()}{vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_frequency\_hz()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_aa498a79da766ce9f30d4518403bfbc96} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+ranging\+\_\+frequency\+\_\+hz (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{frequency\+\_\+hz}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function sets a new ranging frequency in Hz. Ranging frequency corresponds to the measurements frequency. This setting depends of the resolution, so please select your resolution before using this function. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint8\+\_\+t)} & frequency\+\_\+hz \+: Contains the ranging frequency in Hz.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For 4x4, min and max allowed values are \+: \mbox{[}1;60\mbox{]}
\item For 8x8, min and max allowed values are \+: \mbox{[}1;15\mbox{]} 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if ranging frequency is OK, or 127 if the value is not correct. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_mode()}{vl53l8cx\_set\_ranging\_mode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a90f6b7f5130cf36350701771f991bdbf} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+ranging\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{ranging\+\_\+mode}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function is used to set the ranging mode. Two modes are available using ULD \+: Continuous and autonomous. The default mode is Autonomous. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint8\+\_\+t)} & ranging\+\_\+mode \+: Use macros VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+RANGING\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+CONTINUOUS, VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+RANGING\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+CONTINUOUS. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if set ranging mode is OK. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vl53l8cx\_set\_sharpener\_percent()}{vl53l8cx\_set\_sharpener\_percent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_a1a4fb3cfa2082032b917b539e244338a} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+sharpener\+\_\+percent (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{sharpener\+\_\+percent}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function sets a new sharpener value in percent. Sharpener can be changed to blur more or less zones depending of the application. Min value is 0 (disabled), and max is 99. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint32\+\_\+t)} & sharpener\+\_\+percent \+: Value between 0 (disabled) and 99\%. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if set sharpener is OK. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

This function sets a new target order. Please use macros VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+TARGET\+\_\+\+ORDER\+\_\+\+STRONGEST and VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+TARGET\+\_\+\+ORDER\+\_\+\+CLOSEST to define the new output order. By default, the sensor is configured with the strongest output.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if set target order is OK, or 127 if target order is unknown. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+set\+\_\+\+VHV\+\_\+repeat\+\_\+count (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{repeat\+\_\+count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function is used to set a periodic temperature compensation. By setting a repeat count different to 0 the firmware automatically runs a temperature calibration every N frames. default the repeat count is set to 0. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
{\em (uint32\+\_\+t)} & repeat\+\_\+count \+: Number of frames between temperature compensation. Set to 0 to disable the feature (default configuration). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{vl53l8cx__api_8c_ad4cf2ccc4b74c65048046df488da5fce} 
uint8\+\_\+t vl53l8cx\+\_\+stop\+\_\+ranging (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_v_l53_l8_c_x___configuration}{VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+dev}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function stops the ranging session. It must be used when the sensor streams, after calling \doxylink{vl53l8cx__api_8h_aa7a285f38be7f88d2ab894c23e58c8df}{vl53l8cx\+\_\+start\+\_\+ranging()}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em (\+VL53\+L8\+CX\+\_\+\+Configuration)} & \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+\_\+dev \+: VL53\+L8\+CX configuration structure. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
(uint8\+\_\+t) status \+: 0 if stop is OK 
\end{DoxyReturn}
